<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">heremite</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">heremijt</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">eremijt</i>, a borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ecclesiastical_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Ecclesiastical Latin">Ecclesiastical Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">heremita</i>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἐρημίτης</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">erēmítēs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***herenhuis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:herenhuis.html>herenhuis</a> (21609)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heer.html>heer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gentleman, lord</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herenhuis.html>herenhuis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herenhuizen.html>herenhuizen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herenhuis.html>herenhuisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>tall townhouse, often imposing and originally belonging to the elite</li></ol>

***herfst.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:herfst.html>herfst</a> (5103)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:herfst.html>herfst</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*hervist</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*harbistaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kerp-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Herbst</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Harvst</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">hjerst</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">harvest</i>; further with Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">carpere</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pick, to pluck</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Greek <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">καρπός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">karpós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fruit, harvest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The original meaning <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> “harvest time”, as <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> seen in <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herfstmaand.html>herfstmaand</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>autumn, fall</li></ol>

***herinneren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:herinneren.html>herinneren</a> (988)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>16th century, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">erinnern</i>, from late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">erinnern</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herinneren.html>herinneren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remind, prompt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:herinnerde.html>herinnerde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eraan.html>eraan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zondag.html>zondag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She reminded <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> that it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> Sunday.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> ditransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remember, remind oneself
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:herinnerde.html>herinnerde</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naam.html>naam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She no longer remembered my name.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sinds.html>sinds</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:herinneren.html>herinneren</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I have <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> it for as long as I can remember.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herinneren.html>herinneren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to remember</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A memory, something that one remembers.</li>
<li>The act of remembering.</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:herkenbaar.html>herkenbaar</a> (25338)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herkennen.html>herkennen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-baar</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">erkennbar</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herkenbaar.html>herkenbaar</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herkenbaar.html>herkenbaarder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">herkenbaarst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>recognizable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>Geef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:elke.html>elke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groep.html>groep</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:duidelijk.html>duidelijk</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:herkenbare.html>herkenbare</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:naam.html>naam</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Give each group a precise and <b>recognizable</b> name.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hercompst</i>, a derivative of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hercōmen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to come from, originate from</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:her-.html>her-</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:komen.html>komen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-st</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:herleven.html>herleven</a> (16678)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:her-.html>her-</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a></i>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herleven.html>herleven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To come to life again, revive</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To reappear</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To return, rise again</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To recover strength or vitality</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To be renewed</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To relive, experience again</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hermitage.html>hermitage</a> (75431)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">ermitage</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">hermitagium</i>. See <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hermit</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hermitage.html>hermitage</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hermitages</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A house or dwelling where a hermit <a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>lives</a>.</li>
<li>A place of seclusion.</li>
<li>A period of seclusion.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hermitage.html>hermitage</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>  <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>

***hernemen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hernemen.html>hernemen</a> (75430)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:her-.html>her-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">again</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nemen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to take</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***hernia.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hernia.html>hernia</a> (25337)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:hernia.html>hernia</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">protruded viscus</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also yarn and cord.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hernia.html>hernia</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">hernias</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">herniae</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">herniæ</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pathology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A disorder in which a part of the body protrudes abnormally through a tear or opening in an adjacent part, especially of the abdomen.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hernia.html>hernia</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:medisch.html>medisch</a>)</span> uitstulping <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:orgaan.html>orgaan</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:weefsel.html>weefsel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lichaamsholte.html>lichaamsholte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:normaliter.html>normaliter</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:ligt.html>ligt</a></li></ol>

***hersenspoelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hersenspoelen.html>hersenspoelen</a> (27620)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hersenen.html>hersenen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">brain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:spoelen.html>spoelen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rinse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">brainwash</i>, itself a calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chinese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Chinese language">Chinese</a></span> <i class="Hani mention" lang="zh">洗腦／洗脑</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="zh-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xǐnǎo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Some sources consider it a back-formation from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hersenspoeling.html>hersenspoeling</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hersenspoelen.html>hersenspoelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to brainwash

***herstelling.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:herstelling.html>herstelling</a> (51714)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herstellen.html>herstellen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>. First attested in the seventeenth century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herstelling.html>herstelling</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herstellingen.html>herstellingen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>medical recovery, the act or process of healing
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herstel.html>herstel</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>repair, the act or process of fixing an inanimate object
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reparatie.html>reparatie</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>restoration, the act or process of restoring something to its former condition</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:herstelling.html>herstelling</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>

***hert.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hert.html>hert</a> (6817)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hert.html>hert</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hirot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*herutaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ḱerh₂-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hert.html>hert</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herten.html>herten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hertje.html>hertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A deer, a ruminant of the family Cervidae; may occasionally be used of members of the <a href = vnd.unilang:families.html>families</a> <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Moschidae" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Moschidae">Moschidae</a></span> and <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Tragulidae" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Tragulidae">Tragulidae</a></span> in non-scientific use <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">see derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.
<ul><li><b>1773</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:genootschap.html>Genootschap</a> Laus <a href = vnd.unilang:deo.html>Deo</a>, Salus Populo, "Psalm 42" (modernised spelling).
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hijgend.html>Hijgend</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hert.html>hert</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jacht.html>jacht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ontkomen.html>ontkomen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:schreeuwt.html>schreeuwt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sterker.html>sterker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:genot.html>genot</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:frisse.html>frisse</a> waterstromen, <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ziel.html>ziel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verlangt.html>verlangt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a>.</span><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Venison, the meat of a deer.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
